# Overview

Languages

 This table displays the number of **mono-lingual** (or "few"-lingual, with "few" arbitrarily set to 5 or less) **models** and **datasets**, by language. You can click on the figures on the right to the lists of actual
				models and datasets.

**Multilingual** models are listed **here**, while multilingual datasets
				are listed **there**.
